✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅-✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅*✅❌✅—✅❌✅*✅❌✅—✅❌✅P✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅*✅❌✅—✅❌✅*✅❌✅—✅❌✅:✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅P✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅(✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅í✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅,✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅,✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅v✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅,✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅)✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅y✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅á✅❌✅—✅❌✅z✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅p✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅m✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅✅❌✅—✅❌✅

✅❌✅—✅❌✅-✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅[✅❌✅—✅❌✅R✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅C✅❌✅—✅❌✅h✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅]✅❌✅—✅❌✅(✅❌✅—✅❌✅h✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅p✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅:✅❌✅—✅❌✅/✅❌✅—✅❌✅/✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅h✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅g✅❌✅—✅❌✅)✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅—✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅B✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅k✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅h✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅P✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅A✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅g✅❌✅—✅❌✅ü✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅ó✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅h✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅w✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅✅❌✅—✅❌✅
✅❌✅—✅❌✅-✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅[✅❌✅—✅❌✅B✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅T✅❌✅—✅❌✅T✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅]✅❌✅—✅❌✅(✅❌✅—✅❌✅h✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅p✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅:✅❌✅—✅❌✅/✅❌✅—✅❌✅/✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅)✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅—✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅P✅❌✅—✅❌✅l✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅f✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅m✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅v✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅I✅❌✅—✅❌✅A✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅1✅❌✅—✅❌✅1✅❌✅—✅❌✅9✅❌✅—✅❌✅+✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅g✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅✅❌✅—✅❌✅
✅❌✅—✅❌✅-✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅[✅❌✅—✅❌✅G✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅H✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅]✅❌✅—✅❌✅(✅❌✅—✅❌✅h✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅p✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅:✅❌✅—✅❌✅/✅❌✅—✅❌✅/✅❌✅—✅❌✅g✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅h✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅m✅❌✅—✅❌✅/✅❌✅—✅❌✅S✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅c✅❌✅—✅❌✅j✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅)✅❌✅—✅❌✅✅❌✅—✅❌✅
